SELECT `a`.`CartId`, `a`.`ShopperRegId`, `a`.`prod_qty`, `a`.`orderstatus`, `p`.`product_id`, `p`.`product_name`, `p`.`product_subject`, `p`.`product_description`, `p`.`product_image`, `p`.`product_cost`, `b`.`BusinessUsername` AS `StoreName`, `b`.`business_location` AS `StoreLocation`
FROM `addtocart` AS `a`
INNER JOIN `products` AS `p` ON `a`.`product_id` = `p`.`product_id`
